		{
		    var container = $('#codeWindow');
		    if (!container.is(e.target) // if the target of the click isn't the container...

		        container.remove();
		    }
		});

		$(document).ready(function() {
  			
 			
			// // // // // // // // // // // // // // // // // // // // // // // 
			// TRIGGER:
			// change NAV 16-icon in WHITE when selected
			// they must be INSIDE document.ready()
			$('BODY').on('trgActiveDiv', function(e){
  				console.log('>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>><<<<< triggato active div'); console.log(e);
  				try{
  					target = $(e.target).find('SPAN').first().children('img');
  					newImgSrc = target.attr('src').indexOf('-w.png') != -1 ? target.attr('src') : target.attr('src').replace('.png','-w.png');  					
  					target.attr('src', newImgSrc);
				} catch(ex) {
					console.log('img non trovata 2');
				}
			});			
  			$('BODY').on('trgDeActiveDiv', function(e){
  				console.log('####################### triggato DEactive div'); console.log(e);
  				try{
  					target = $(e.target).find('SPAN').first().children('img');
  					newImgSrc = target.attr('src').replace('-w.png','.png');  					
  					target.attr('src', newImgSrc);
				} catch(ex) {
					console.log('img non trovata 2');
				}
			});				
			// // // // // // // // // // // // // // // // // // // // // // // 	 			
 			
			loadingScreen('loading');

			// Hide Section			
			$('.partDiv').hide();
			$('.chapterDiv').hide();
			$('.sectionDiv').hide();			
		
			// Show current Chapter
			var pageSection = $('div#pageInfo').attr('pagesection');
			var pageClass 	= $('div#pageInfo').attr('pageclass');
			var pageId 		= $('div#pageInfo').attr('pageid');			
			var pageVolume 	= $('div#pageInfo').attr('pagevolume');			
			var exerciseId 	= $('div#pageInfo').attr('exerciseid');	
			var thisDiv 	= $('DIV#nav DIV[section="' + pageSection + '"]');			
  			
  			// On Loading:
			if(thisDiv.attr('class') == 'sectionToc'){
				// Se ha un chapterDiv
				if(thisDiv.parent('.chapterDiv').length) {				
					thisDiv.parent('.chapterDiv').show();
					thisDiv.parent('.chapterDiv').parent('.partDiv').show();
					thisDiv.find('img').attr('src', 'icons/16-contract.png');	
					thisDiv.parent('.chapterDiv').prev('.chapterToc').find('img').attr('src', 'icons/16-contract.png');	
					thisDiv.parent('.chapterDiv').parent('.partDiv').prev('.partToc').find('img').attr('src', 'icons/16-contract.png');	
					thisDiv.next('.sectionDiv').show();	
				} 
				// SE non ha un chapterDiv
				else {
					thisDiv.parent('.partDiv').show();
					thisDiv.find('img').attr('src', 'icons/16-contract.png');
					thisDiv.parent('.partDiv').prev('.partToc').find('img').attr('src', 'icons/16-contract.png');	
					thisDiv.next('.sectionDiv').show();					
				}
				
				// We are into Subsection:
				if(window.location.hash && $('DIV#nav A[hash="' + window.location.hash + '"]').length ){				
					highlightSubsection();
				}	
				// We are into Section:
				else {
					thisDiv.children('a').addClass('active');
					thisDiv.wrap('<div class="activeDiv"></div>').trigger('trgActiveDiv');		
				}					
			}
			
			if(thisDiv.attr('class') == 'chapterToc'){
				thisDiv.parent('.partDiv').show();
				thisChapter = $('DIV#nav DIV[id="chapterId241"]');
				thisChapter.children('a').addClass('active');
				thisChapter.wrap('<div class="activeDiv"></div>').trigger('trgActiveDiv');				
			}
			
			if(thisDiv.attr('class') == 'partToc'){
				thisChapter = $('DIV#nav DIV[section="' + pageSection + '"]').not('.chapterToc');
				thisChapter.children('a').addClass('active');
				thisChapter.addClass('activeDiv');
				thisChapter.trigger('trgActiveDiv');
				//$('BODY').trigger('trgActiveDiv');
				//$('BODY').on('trgActiveDiv', function() {console.log('22222222222222222222222 trgActiveDiv');});
			}	
		
			//////////////////////////////////////////// REMOVE EXPAND/COLLAPSE ICONS IF EMPTY:
			$('DIV.chapterToc').each(function(i){
				// if ACTIVE this is wrapped by DIV.activeDiv
				if( $(this).parent('DIV.activeDiv').length == 1 )
					thisElem = $(this).parent('DIV.activeDiv');
				else
					thisElem = $(this);
					
				if( thisElem.next('DIV.chapterDiv').length == 0 ) {
					thisElem.find('img').prop('src', '/lab/icons/16-empty.png');
					thisElem.find('img').css('cursor', 'default');
					thisElem.find('span.chapterExpand').removeClass('chapterExpand');
				}				
			});
			$('DIV.sectionToc').each(function(i){
				// if ACTIVE this is wrapped by DIV.activeDiv
				if( $(this).parent('DIV.activeDiv').length == 1 )
					thisElem = $(this).parent('DIV.activeDiv');
				else
					thisElem = $(this);
					
				if( thisElem.next('DIV.sectionDiv').length == 0 ) {
					thisElem.find('img').prop('src', '/lab/icons/16-empty.png');
					thisElem.find('img').css('cursor', 'default');
					thisElem.find('span.chapterExpand').removeClass('chapterExpand');
				}				
			});

				$('#nav').find('A.active').removeClass('active');

				highlightSubsection(hash);

			// Per Ajax:

				$('#nav').find('.activeDiv DIV').unwrap().trigger('trgDeActiveDiv');		
				$('#nav').find('.activeDiv').removeClass('activeDiv').trigger('trgDeActiveDiv');		
				$('#nav').find('A.active').removeClass('active');		
				$(this).addClass('active');
				//$(this).parent('DIV').wrap('<div class="activeDiv"></div>');
				$(this).parent('DIV').wrap('<div class="activeDiv"></div>').trigger('trgActiveDiv');
			});
			$('DIV.partToc A').on('click', function(){
				$('#nav').find('.activeDiv DIV').unwrap().trigger('trgDeActiveDiv');		
				$('#nav').find('.activeDiv').removeClass('activeDiv').trigger('trgDeActiveDiv');		
				$('#nav').find('A.active').removeClass('active');	
				$(this).addClass('active');	
				//$(this).parent('DIV.partToc').addClass('activeDiv');
				$(this).parent('DIV.partToc').addClass('activeDiv').trigger('trgActiveDiv');
				
				//$(this).parent('DIV').wrap('<div class="activeDiv"></div>');
			});			
	 
			// Expand Chapter:
			$('.chapterExpand').on('click', function(){
				if( $(this).parent('div.partToc').attr('section') == 'masterT' || $(this).parent('div.partToc').attr('section') == 'masterE' ) {
					var divToToggle = $(this).parent().next('.godToc');
					ph = 1;
				}
				else {
					if( $(this).attr('type') == 'partToc' ){
						var divToToggle = $(this).parent().next('.partDiv');
						ph = 2;
					}  
					else if ( $(this).parent('div.sectionToc').length ) {
						if($(this).parents('.activeDiv').length){
							var divToToggle = $(this).parent().parent().next('.sectionDiv');
							ph = 5;
						}
						else {
							var divToToggle = $(this).parent().next('.sectionDiv');
							ph = 6;
						}						
					}
					else {
						if($(this).parents('.activeDiv').length){
							var divToToggle = $(this).parent().parent().next('.chapterDiv');
							ph = 3;							
						}
						else {
							var divToToggle = $(this).parent().next('.chapterDiv');
							ph = 4;
						}
					}
				}
				console.log(divToToggle);
				console.log("PH:" + ph);				
				
				if(divToToggle.is(':hidden')){
					divToToggle.show('fast');
					imgName = $(this).children('img').attr('src').indexOf('-w.png') != -1 ? '16-contract-w.png' : '16-contract.png'; console.log('@@@@@@@@@@@@@ 1' + imgName);
					$(this).children('img').attr('src', 'icons/' + imgName);
				} else {
					divToToggle.hide('fast');
					imgName = $(this).children('img').attr('src').indexOf('-w.png') != -1 ? '16-expand-w.png' : '16-expand.png'; console.log('@@@@@@@@@@@@@ 2' + imgName);
					$(this).children('img').attr('src', 'icons/' + imgName);
				}
			});

						$('#main').css('width','65%');
						$('#main').css('margin-left','30%');
						navStatus = 'open';

			//////////////////////////////////////////// Take screenshot
			$('BODY').on('click', '#takeScreenshot', function(e){
				e.preventDefault();
				$('#divFeedbackInfo').css('visibility', 'hidden');
				$('BODY').css('cursor', 'wait').append('<div id="tmpWait" style="position:fixed; top:0px; left:0px; z-index:10000; background:red; color:#fff; font:12px sans-serif;"><img src="/lab/icons/loading.gif" class="newIcon24" />...WAIT...SCREENSHOT IN PROGRESS...</div>');
				
				//$('#takeScreenshot').replaceWith('<span style="float:left"><div id="screenshotLoading" style="text-align:center; margin:0 20px;"><img src="/lab/icons/loading.gif" class="newIcon24" /></div></span>');
				html2canvas(document.body).then(function(canvas) {
            		//document.body.appendChild(canvas);
            		$(canvas).width(100);
            		$(canvas).height(100);
            		$(canvas).css( {'border': 			'3px solid rgb(60, 149, 145)', 
            						'position': 		'relative',
            						'top': 				'-180px',
            						'background-color': '#fff'				
            		});
            		$('#divFeedbackInfo').append(canvas);            		
            		$('#takeScreenshot').hide();
            		//$('#screenshotLoading').hide();
            		
            		$('#divFeedbackInfo').css('visibility', 'visible');
            		$('BODY').css('cursor', 'pointer');
            		$('#tmpWait').remove();
        		});
			});
		  	//////////////////////////////////////////// Send Feedback/Message: 
		  	function sendFeedback($formData){
		  			try {
						$.ajax({
							method: 'POST',	
  		  					url: '/lab/xhr/sendMessage.srv.php',
  							//data: 'message=' + message
  							data: $formData,
		    				contentType: false, // NEEDED, DON'T OMIT THIS 
		    				processData: false, // NEEDED, DON'T OMIT THIS  						
				  		})
  				   		.done(function( msg ) {
  				   			msg = msg + '<br /><br /><div id="divFeedbackInfoClose" style="cursor:pointer">Click here to close this window.</div><br /><div id="divFeedbackInfoResend" style="cursor:pointer">Click here to send another message.</div>';
    	   					$('#divFeedbackInfoUpName').html(msg);
    	   					$('DIV#divFeedbackInfoDownButton').hide();
    	   					// Clean:
    	   					if ($('canvas').length) $('canvas').remove();
    	   					$('INPUT#feedbackFiles').hide();
  	  			   		})  	  			   
  				   		.fail(function( msg ) {
    	   					$('#divFeedbackInfoUpName').html('<div style="text-align:center">Something went wrong :-(<br>Please retry later.</div>');
  	  			   		}); 
  	  			   		
					} catch(ex) {
						$('#divFeedbackInfoUpName').html('<div style="text-align:center">Something went wrong :-(<br>Please retry later.</div>');
					}				  		
			}
						
		  	$('BODY').on('click', 'DIV#divFeedbackInfoDown A', function(e){
		  		
		  		var message = $('#txtaFeedbackInfoUpMessage').val();
		  		
		  		if(!message) { alert('Write something...'); return false; }
		  		
		  		e.preventDefault();
		  		
		  		$('#divFeedbackInfoUpName').html('<div style="text-align:center"><img src="/lab/icons/loading.gif" class="newIcon64" /></div>');
		  		
		  		var $formData = new FormData( $('#frmFeedback')[0] ); // serve: [0]				
				$formData.append('message', message);	// appendo a mano, con new non lo prende.		
				            
		  		var canvas = document.getElementsByTagName("CANVAS")[0];
				if (canvas !== undefined && canvas.toBlob) {
					
					canvas.toBlob(function (blob) {
						
						setTimeout(function () {     
							$formData.append('fileCanvas', blob, 'screenshot.jpg');	
							// 'of' is not supported in IE9, enable only for debug purpose
							//for(var pair of $formData.entries()) {
							//	console.log("dentro" + pair[0]+ ', '+ pair[1]); 
							//}
							
							sendFeedback($formData); 
						}, 5000);
						
					},'image/jpeg');
					
				} else { 
						console.log("2000");
	  					sendFeedback($formData);
				}  		
		  		
			});

				  	positionToAppend 	= 'DIV#main';
				  	newHeightRel 		= $(this).offset().top - 90;
				  	newRight 			= '';
				}

					permalink 			= 'https://bet.arpm.co/lab/redirect.php?videoplay=' + $(this).attr('permalink');
				  	positionToAppend 	= 'DIV#main';
				  	newHeightRel 		= $(this).offset().top - 90;
				  	newRight 			= '';
				}
				else if( $(this).hasClass('permaVideoplayOverlay') ) {
					permalink 			= 'https://bet.arpm.co/lab/redirect.php?videoplay=' + $(this).attr('permalink');
					positionToAppend 	= 'DIV#videoDiv .mfp-title';
					newHeightRel 		= -50;
					newRight 			= 0;
				} 
				else if( $(this).hasClass('permaSlideplay') ) {
					permalink 			= 'https://bet.arpm.co/lab/redirect.php?slideplay=' + $(this).attr('permalink');
				  	positionToAppend 	= 'DIV#main';
				  	newHeightRel 		= $(this).offset().top - 90;
				  	newRight 			= '';
				}
				else if( $(this).hasClass('permaSlideplayOverlay') ) {
					permalink 			= 'https://bet.arpm.co/lab/redirect.php?slideplay=' + $(this).attr('permalink');
					positionToAppend 	= 'DIV#slideDiv .mfp-title';
					newHeightRel 		= -50;
					newRight 			= 0;
				}
				else if( $(this).hasClass('permaLectureplay') ) {
					permalink 			= 'https://bet.arpm.co/lab/redirect.php?lectureplay=' + $(this).attr('permalink');
					positionToAppend 	= 'DIV#main';
					newHeightRel 		= $(this).offset().top - 90;
					newRight 			= 0;
				}				
				else if( $(this).hasClass('permaLectureplayOverlay') ) {
					permalink 			= 'https://bet.arpm.co/lab/redirect.php?lectureplay=' + $(this).attr('permalink');
					positionToAppend 	= 'DIV#lectureDiv .mfp-title';
					newHeightRel 		= -50;
					newRight 			= 0;
				}				
				else {
					permalink 			= 'https://bet.arpm.co/lab/redirect.php?permalink=' + $(this).attr('permalink');	//permalink = 'https://bet.arpm.co/lab/' + encodeURI($(this).attr('permalink')) + '.html';				  
				  	positionToAppend 	= 'DIV#main';
				  	newHeightRel 		= $(this).offset().top - 90;
				  	newRight 			= '';
				}
				
				$('#popup-permalink').html(permalink);
				$('#cpClipboard').text(permalink); // mantenere il div da copiare fuori dal div da detachare.

				e.stopPropagation();
				if($(window).width() < 767) {
					$(this).after( $( ".popup" ) );
					$('.popup').show().addClass('popup-mobile').css('top', 0);

					$('html, body').animate({
						scrollTop: $('.popup').offset().top
					}, 500);   

				} 
				else {
					$('.popup').removeClass('popup-mobile').css('top', newHeightRel).toggle();
					$('.popup').css('right', newRight);
				};
				
				/* I permalink sugli overlay devono essere dentro l'overlay */
				$('.popup').detach().appendTo(positionToAppend);				
			});

  			//////////// CODE MINIWINDOW PYTHON/OCTAVE:
			$('DIV#main').on('click', '.code-zoom', function(e){
					
					var oIcon = $(this);
					e.preventDefault();
					$.ajax({
						method: 'GET',
						url: 'xhr/getCodeLang.srv.php',
						data: 'code=' + getQueryVariable('code', extractQueryString($(this).attr('href'), false))
					})
					.done(function( msg ) {
						var aCodeFlag = msg.split('::::');
				 		codeWindow = '<div id="codeWindow" style="width:300px; height:120px; position:absolute; background:#3c9591; color:#fff; box-shadow:2px 2px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.5); border:1px solid #aaa; padding:5px; box-sizing:border-box; z-index:10">' +
				 					 '	<div style="float:right; font:12px Ubuntu, sans-serif; font-weight:bold; cursor:pointer; position:absolute; right:5px; " onclick="$(this).parent().remove()">X</div>' +
				 					 '	<div style="clear:both; height:9px;"></div>' +
				 					 (aCodeFlag[0] == 1 ? '	<div style="display:inline-block; text-align:center; width:56%; vertical-align:top; "><a href="' + oIcon.attr('href') +'&codeLang=Octave" class="light code-jhub" target="_blank"><img src="/lab/icons/icon_w_matlab.png" class="newIcon48"><img src="/lab/icons/icon_w_octave2.png" class="newIcon48"><br /><small style="display:blocK; line-height:16px; margin-top:10px;">MATLAB -<br />GNU Octave</small></a></div>':'') +
				 					 (aCodeFlag[1] == 1 ? '	<div style="display:inline-block; text-align:center; width:33%; vertical-align:top; "><a href="' + oIcon.attr('href') +'&codeLang=Python" class="light code-jhub" target="_blank"><img src="/lab/icons/icon_w_python2.png" class="newIcon64"><br />Python</a></div>':'') +
				 					 '	<div class="arrow-right" style="position:absolute; top:40px; right:-20px; border-left-color:#3c9591; border-width:20px; "></div>' +
				 					 '</div>';   	 
				 					 
				 				 
				 		if($('#codeWindow').length)	$('#codeWindow').remove();
				 		else 				 		$('BODY').append(codeWindow); //$(this).parent().append(codeWindow);
				 		
				 		// Se ci sono piu icone nella stessa pagina, devo differenziare quella su cui ho fatto click: aggiungo attr rel=code-clicked
				 		$('.code-zoom').removeAttr('rel');
				 		oIcon.attr('rel', 'code-clicked');
				 		
				 		
				 		//posSomething( $('#codeWindow'), $('A.code-zoom IMG'), oPosParams = {top:-40, left:-280} );
				 		if(oIcon.children('IMG').hasClass('shiftDown'))	  		oPosParams = {top:20,  left:-280};
				 		else if(oIcon.children('IMG').hasClass('shiftDown40'))	oPosParams = {top:0,   left:-280};
				 		else if(oIcon.children('IMG').hasClass('shiftDown50'))	oPosParams = {top:10,  left:-280};
				 		else if(oIcon.children('IMG').hasClass('shiftDown60'))	oPosParams = {top:20,  left:-280};
				 		else if(oIcon.children('IMG').hasClass('shiftDown70'))	oPosParams = {top:30,  left:-280};
				 		else if(oIcon.children('IMG').hasClass('shiftDown80'))	oPosParams = {top:40,  left:-280};
				 		else													oPosParams = {top:-40, left:-280};
				 		
						//posSomething( $('#codeWindow'), $('A.code-zoom IMG'), oPosParams = $(this).children('IMG').hasClass('shiftDown') ? {top:20, left:-280} : {top:-40, left:-280});
						posSomething( $('#codeWindow'), $('A.code-zoom[rel="code-clicked"] IMG'), oPosParams);				 					 
					})  	  			   
					.fail(function( msg ) {
					    alert( 'Error: ' + msg + "\n" + 'Try to reload the web page' );
					});						
					


			});

			$('DIV#main').on('click', '.slide-zoom, .video-zoom, .lecture-zoom', function(e){
				
					e.preventDefault();
					
					if($(this).attr('class') == 'slide-zoom'){
						resType		= 's';
						param 		= 'slide';
						dir 		= 'slides';
						divName 	= 'slideDiv';
						style 		= 'width:70%; height:70%; padding:5%;text-align:center;';
						titleOnRight= '<div style="text-align:right; float:right; margin-right:20px;">' + 
																				'<b title="Close" id="btnOverlayClose" class="fancybox-close" ></b>' + 
									   '</div>';	//<!-- <img src="/lab/icons/icon_close3.png" class="newIcon16" id="btnOverlayClose" alt="Close" title="Close" /> -->
					}
					//else if($(this).attr('class') == 'video-zoom'){
					else if($(this).hasClass('video-zoom')){
						resType		= 'v';
						param 		= 'video';
						dir 		= 'videos';
						divName 	= 'videoDiv';						
						style 		= 'width:70%; height:70%; padding:5%;';
						titleOnRight= '<div style="text-align:right; float:right; margin-right:20px;">' +
																				'<b title="Close" id="btnOverlayClose" class="fancybox-close" ></b>' +
									   '</div>'; //<img src="/lab/icons/icon_close3.png" class="newIcon16" id="btnOverlayClose" alt="Close" title="Close" />
					}
					else if($(this).hasClass('lecture-zoom')){
						resType		= 'l';
						param 		= 'lecture';
						dir 		= 'lectures';
						divName 	= 'lectureDiv';						
						style 		= 'width:70%; height:70%; padding:5%;';
						titleOnRight= '<div style="text-align:right; float:right; margin-right:20px;">' +
																				'<b title="Close" id="btnOverlayClose" class="fancybox-close" ></b>' +
									   '</div>'; //<img src="/lab/icons/icon_close3.png" class="newIcon16" id="btnOverlayClose" alt="Close" title="Close" />
					}
					
					permalink = getQueryVariable(param, extractQueryString($(this).attr('href'), false));
					
					$.ajax({
						method: 'GET',
						url: 'xhr/getResource.srv.php',
						data: 'permalink=' + permalink + '&resType=' + resType
					})
					.done(function( msg ) {
						//vimeoMutex = 'load';
						resData = msg.split('::::'); // [0] => link, [1] => iframe full code, [2] => title, [3] => DL URL

						overlayCode = 	 '<div id="' + divName + '" class="mfp-hide" style="text-align:center;margin:0 auto;' + style +'">' +
					    				 '	<div class="mfp-title" style="background:#3c9591; padding:5px; font:14px Ubuntu, sans-serif; text-shadow:1px 1px 1px #000; position:relative; "><strong>' + urldecode(resData[2]) + '</strong>' +
					    				 '	' + titleOnRight.replace(/\[##PERMALINK##\]/g, permalink) +
					    				 '	</div>' +
					    				 '	<div class="embed-container">' + urldecode(resData[1]) + '</div>' +
					    				 '</div>';
					    $('body').append(overlayCode);
						$.magnificPopup.open({
									items: {src:'#' + divName},
									type: 'inline',
									showCloseBtn: false,
									callbacks: { close: destroyMagnificpopup}
								}, 0);
					   $('#' + divName).draggable();

					})
					.fail(function( msg ) {
					    alert( "Error: " + msg );
					});	
					
					   			
					return false;
			});

			function destroyMagnificpopup(){

				console.log('f(x) destroyMagnificpopup: CLOSE POPUP OVERLAY');
				
				// Rimetto popup al suo posto
				$('.popup').detach().appendTo('DIV#main');
 
				$.magnificPopup.close();	
				$('#videoDiv').remove();	//rimuove le copie che fa dei div (e che le sposta)
				$('#slideDiv').remove();				
				$('#lectureDiv').remove();		
				
			}

      <div class="popupHighBorder">
       PRIVACY POLICY
      </div> 
      <div class="popupContent" id="privacyChrome"> 
       <br>Last Modified: February 1, 2016 
       <br> 
       <br> 
       <br>Our Commitment to Privacy 
       <br> 
       <br>ARPMs Privacy Policy was developed as an extension of our commitment to combine the highest-quality products and services with the highest level of integrity in dealing with our clients and partners. The Policy is designed to help you understand how we collect, use, and safeguard the personal information you provide to us and to help you make informed decisions when using our site and our products and services. This statement will be continuously assessed against new technologies, business practices, and our customers needs. 
       <br> 
       <br>Personal information means data that allows someone to identify or contact you, including, for example, your name, address, telephone number, email address, as well as any other non-public information that is associated with or linked to any of the foregoing data. This Privacy Policy describes the treatment of information provided or collected on all linked pages owned and operated by ARPM, LLC (ARPM) and the ARPM Service (Services). This Policy is referenced in, and is an integral part of, the Terms of Service governing the ARPM website (the Website). 
       <br> 
       <br>We collect two basic types of information: data that you provide (User-Provided Data) and data collected via technology (Website Collected Information). We may use both types of data to create Anonymous Data. 
       <br> 
       <br>User-Provided Data 
       <br> 
       <br>ARPM requires certain personal information to enable registration, including your name and email address. If you participate in a course of study through the Website, or if your course of study is subsidized in part or in full by a third party with whom you are affiliated (Sponsoring Organization), then this information might be provided on your behalf by that institution. Other data that you provide by populating profile information or by using Website features, including all chats, posts, images, or other user inputs, are not required for Service usage and therefore are considered to be disclosed publicly and provided voluntarily. 
       <br> 
       <br>In the event that you purchase a product or service through ARPM, including but not limited to licenses to electronic books, courses, or other content, we may collect transaction information such as your postal address or certain payment information. We use a third-party intermediary to manage credit card processing, and your credit card information is securely transmitted to that intermediary directly. Your full credit card number is never transmitted to or viewed by anyone at ARPM. However, we are given and may print a portion of your credit card information on your receipt to let you know which credit card you used to make a purchase. Except to process your credit card information for current or future purchases through ARPM, this intermediary processor is not permitted to store, retain, or use your billing information. If we ever terminate the agreement with our current vendor, then information may be transferred to another certified payment processor. 
       <br> 
       <br>Website-Collected Data 
       <br> 
       <br>We may also collect some information that you dont type in yourself, through the use of cookies and other software technologies such as Linked-In. In the case of data obtained through Linked-In, we only collect your name, photo, headline, current positions, and primary email address. 
       <br> 
       <br>Cookies are a feature of web browser software that allows web servers to recognize the computer used to access a website. They are small pieces of data that are stored by a users web browser on the users hard drive. Cookies can remember what information a user accesses on one web page to simplify subsequent interactions with that website by the same user or to use the information to streamline the users transactions on related web pages. This makes it easier for a user to move from web page to web page and to complete commercial transactions over the Internet. 
       <br> 
       <br>Like other Internet services, we automatically gather cookie data and store it in data stores each time you access the Website. The username that you use to log in to the system is stored in cookies on your computer. If you turn cookies off, you will not be able to use our Website. Cookies should make your online experience easier and more personalized. 
       <br> 
       <br>Our servers collect such information as your IP address, the type of computer operating system youre using, which device and web browser youre using, the frequency with which you visit parts of the Website, and other usage or technical data. This information is used to maintain and improve the internal operations of the Website. 
       <br> 
       <br>Customized Learning Experience

This data may be stored and analyzed in order to best tailor the Service to your individual needs. If you participate in a course of study with an educational institution or a Sponsoring Organization through the Website, then this data may be shared with that organization to facilitate teaching and evaluation.
